            Type = Clothing,
            Cosmetic = TRUE,
            DisplayName = Cosmetic Dress,
            ClothingItem = Belt,
            BodyLocation = Transmog_Dress,
            Icon = DressMediumWhite,
            Weight = 0,
        }

        recipe Get Cosmetic Dress
        {
            keep Base.Dress_Normal,

            Result:TransmogV2.Base_Dress_Normal,
            Time:30.0,
            Category:Transmog,
        }

        recipe Hide Dress
        {
            keep Base.Dress_Normal,

            Result:TransmogV2.Hide_Dress,
            Time:30.0,
            Category:Transmog - Hide,
        }
